   28 /*  Table mlib_filters_u8_bl
   29  *
   30  *  DESCRIPTION
   31  *    mlib_filters_u8_bl[i].s[0] = mlib_filters_u8_bl[i + 256].s[0] = (511 - 2*i) << SHIFT;
   32  *    mlib_filters_u8_bl[i].s[2] = mlib_filters_u8_bl[i + 256].s[1] = (511 - 2*i) << SHIFT;
   33  *    mlib_filters_u8_bl[i].s[1] = mlib_filters_u8_bl[i + 256].s[2] = (2*i + 1) << SHIFT;
   34  *    mlib_filters_u8_bl[i].s[3] = mlib_filters_u8_bl[i + 256].s[3] = (2*i + 1) << SHIFT;
   35  *
   36  *  Where
   37  *    SHIFT = 5;
   38  *    i = 0, 1, ..., 255;
   39  *
   40  *  Tables mlib_filters_u8_bc and mlib_filters_u8_bc2
   41  *
   42  *  DESCRIPTION
   43  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc[i].s[0] = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
   44  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc[i].s[1] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
   45  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc[i].s[2] = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
   46  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc[i].s[3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
   47  *
   48  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2[i].s[0] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
   49  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2[i].s[1] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
   50  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2[i].s[2] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
   51  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2[i].s[3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
   52  *
   53  *  Where
   54  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 14));
   55  *    dx = (double)i/256 + 1./512.; i = 0, 1, ..., 255;
   56  *
   57  *  Tables mlib_filters_u8_bc_3 and mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3
   58  *
   59  *  DESCRIPTION
   60  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i].s[0-2]   = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
   61  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i].s[3]     =
   62  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i+1].s[0-1] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
   63  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i+1].s[2-3] =
   64  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i+2].s[0]   = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
   65  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_3[3*i+2].s[1-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
   66  *
   67  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i].s[0-2]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
   68  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i].s[3]     =
   69  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i+1].s[0-1] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
   70  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i+1].s[2-3] =
   71  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i+2].s[0]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
   72  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_3[3*i+2].s[1-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
   73  *
   74  *  Where
   75  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 14));
   76  *    dx = (double)i/256 + 1./512.; i = 0, 1, ..., 255;
   77  *
   78  *  Tables mlib_filters_u8_bc_4 and mlib_filters_u8_bc2_4
   79  *
   80  *  DESCRIPTION
   81  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_4[4*i].s[0-3]   = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
   82  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_4[4*i+1].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
   83  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_4[4*i+2].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
   84  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc_4[4*i+3].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
   85  *
   86  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_4[4*i].s[0-3]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
   87  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_4[4*i+1].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
   88  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_4[4*i+2].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
   89  *    mlib_filters_u8_bc2_4[4*i+3].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
   90  *
   91  *  Where
   92  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 14));
   93  *    dx = (double)i/256 + 1./512.; i = 0, 1, ..., 255;
   94  *
   95  *  Tables mlib_filters_s16_bc and mlib_filters_s16_bc2
   96  *
   97  *  DESCRIPTION
   98  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc[i].s[0] = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
   99  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc[i].s[1] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
  100  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc[i].s[2] = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
  101  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc[i].s[3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
  102  *
  103  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2[i].s[0] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
  104  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2[i].s[1] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
  105  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2[i].s[2] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
  106  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2[i].s[3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
  107  *
  108  *  Where
  109  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 15));
  110  *    dx = (double)i/512 + 1./1024.; i = 0, 1, ..., 511;
  111  *    All 32768 are replace to 32767
  112  *
  113  *  Tables mlib_filters_s16_bc_3 and mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3
  114  *
  115  *  DESCRIPTION
  116  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i].s[0-2]   = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
  117  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i].s[3]     =
  118  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i+1].s[0-1] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
  119  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i+1].s[2-3] =
  120  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i+2].s[0]   = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
  121  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_3[3*i+2].s[1-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
  122  *
  123  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i].s[0-2]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
  124  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i].s[3]     =
  125  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i+1].s[0-1] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
  126  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i+1].s[2-3] =
  127  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i+2].s[0]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
  128  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_3[3*i+2].s[1-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
  129  *
  130  *  Where
  131  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 15));
  132  *    dx = (double)i/512 + 1./1024.; i = 0, 1, ..., 511;
  133  *    All 32768 are replace to 32767
  134  *
  135  *  Tables mlib_filters_s16_bc_4 and mlib_filters_s16_bc2_4
  136  *
  137  *  DESCRIPTION
  138  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_4[4*i].s[0-3]   = (mlib_s16) ((-0.5*dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx - 0.5*dx)*PREC - 0.5);
  139  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_4[4*i+1].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 1.5*dx*dx*dx - 2.5*dx*dx + 1.0   )*PREC + 0.5);
  140  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_4[4*i+2].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) ((-1.5*dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx + 0.5*dx)*PREC + 0.5);
  141  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc_4[4*i+3].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( 0.5*dx*dx*dx - 0.5*dx*dx         )*PREC - 0.5);
  142  *
  143  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_4[4*i].s[0-3]   = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx + 2.0*dx*dx - dx )*PREC - 0.5);
  144  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_4[4*i+1].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx - 2.0*dx*dx + 1.0)*PREC + 0.5);
  145  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_4[4*i+2].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) ((-dx*dx*dx +     dx*dx + dx )*PREC + 0.5);
  146  *    mlib_filters_s16_bc2_4[4*i+3].s[0-3] = (mlib_s16) (( dx*dx*dx -     dx*dx      )*PREC - 0.5);
  147  *
  148  *  Where
  149  *    PREC = ((double) (1 << 15));
  150  *    dx = (double)i/512 + 1./1024.; i = 0, 1, ..., 511;
  151  *    All 32768 are replace to 32767
  152  *
  153  *  COMMENTS
  154  *    These tables are used by VIS versions of the following functions:
